\documentclass[11pt]{article}

    
    
    \usepackage[T1]{fontenc}
    % Nicer default font (+ math font) than Computer Modern for most use cases
    \usepackage{mathpazo}

    % Basic figure setup, for now with no caption control since it's done
    % automatically by Pandoc (which extracts ![](path) syntax from Markdown).
    \usepackage{graphicx}
    % We will generate all images so they have a width \maxwidth. This means
    % that they will get their normal width if they fit onto the page, but
    % are scaled down if they would overflow the margins.
    \makeatletter
    \def\maxwidth{\ifdim\Gin@nat@width>\linewidth\linewidth
    \else\Gin@nat@width\fi}
    \makeatother
    \let\Oldincludegraphics\includegraphics
    % Set max figure width to be 80% of text width, for now hardcoded.
    \renewcommand{\includegraphics}[1]{\Oldincludegraphics[width=.8\maxwidth]{#1}}
    % Ensure that by default, figures have no caption (until we provide a
    % proper Figure object with a Caption API and a way to capture that
    % in the conversion process - todo).
    \usepackage{caption}
    \DeclareCaptionLabelFormat{nolabel}{}
    \captionsetup{labelformat=nolabel}

    \usepackage{adjustbox} % Used to constrain images to a maximum size 
    \usepackage{xcolor} % Allow colors to be defined
    \usepackage{enumerate} % Needed for markdown enumerations to work
    \usepackage{geometry} % Used to adjust the document margins
    \usepackage{amsmath} % Equations
    \usepackage{amssymb} % Equations
    \usepackage{textcomp} % defines textquotesingle
    % Hack from http://tex.stackexchange.com/a/47451/13684:
    \AtBeginDocument{%
        \def\PYZsq{\textquotesingle}% Upright quotes in Pygmentized code
    }
    \usepackage{upquote} % Upright quotes for verbatim code
    \usepackage{eurosym} % defines \euro
    \usepackage[mathletters]{ucs} % Extended unicode (utf-8) support
    \usepackage[utf8x]{inputenc} % Allow utf-8 characters in the tex document
    \usepackage{fancyvrb} % verbatim replacement that allows latex
    \usepackage{grffile} % extends the file name processing of package graphics 
                         % to support a larger range 
    % The hyperref package gives us a pdf with properly built
    % internal navigation ('pdf bookmarks' for the table of contents,
    % internal cross-reference links, web links for URLs, etc.)
    \usepackage{hyperref}
    \usepackage{longtable} % longtable support required by pandoc >1.10
    \usepackage{booktabs}  % table support for pandoc > 1.12.2
    \usepackage[inline]{enumitem} % IRkernel/repr support (it uses the enumerate* environment)
    \usepackage[normalem]{ulem} % ulem is needed to support strikethroughs (\sout)
                                % normalem makes italics be italics, not underlines

\def\PY@reset{\let\PY@it=\relax \let\PY@bf=\relax%
    \let\PY@ul=\relax \let\PY@tc=\relax%
    \let\PY@bc=\relax \let\PY@ff=\relax}

    \section{26. Remove Duplicates from Sorted
Array}\label{remove-duplicates-from-sorted-array}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}1}]:} \PY{k}{class} \PY{n+nc}{Solution}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{object}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{removeDuplicates}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{nums}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                \PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
        \PY{l+s+sd}{        :type nums: List[int]}
        \PY{l+s+sd}{        :rtype: int}
        \PY{l+s+sd}{        \PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
                \PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{nums}\PY{p}{)}
                \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{:} \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{n}
                \PY{n}{i} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}
                \PY{n}{j} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}
                \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{j} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{range}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{n}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{nums}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{j}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{!=}\PY{n}{nums}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{:} 
                        \PY{n}{i}\PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}
                        \PY{n}{nums}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{nums}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{j}\PY{p}{]}
                \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{i}\PY{o}{+}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}
                    
\end{Verbatim}

    \section{27. Remove Element}\label{remove-element}

                     \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{word} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{locations}\PY{p}{:}
                         \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{locations}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{word}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{]}
                     \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
                         \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{locations}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{word}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{)}
                 
         
             \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{shortest}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{word1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{word2}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                 \PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
         \PY{l+s+sd}{        :type word1: str}
         \PY{l+s+sd}{        :type word2: str}
         \PY{l+s+sd}{        :rtype: int}
         \PY{l+s+sd}{        \PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
                 \PY{n}{loc1} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{locations}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{word1}\PY{p}{]}
                 \PY{n}{loc2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{locations}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{word2}\PY{p}{]}
                 \PY{n}{i} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}
                 \PY{n}{j} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}
                 \PY{n}{minD} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{float}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{inf}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
                 \PY{k}{while} \PY{n}{i}\PY{o}{\PYZlt{}}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{loc1}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o+ow}{and} \PY{n}{j}\PY{o}{\PYZlt{}}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{loc2}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                     \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{loc1}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{n}{loc2}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{j}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{:}
                         \PY{n}{minD} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{min}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{minD}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{loc1}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{n}{loc2}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{j}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
                         \PY{n}{j}\PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}
                     \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
                         \PY{n}{minD} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{min}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{minD}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{loc2}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{j}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{n}{loc1}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
                         \PY{n}{i}\PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}
                 \PY{k}{while} \PY{n}{i}\PY{o}{\PYZlt{}}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{loc1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                     \PY{n}{minD} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{min}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{minD}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n+nb}{abs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{loc1}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{n}{loc2}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
                     \PY{n}{i}\PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}
                 \PY{k}{while} \PY{n}{j}\PY{o}{\PYZlt{}}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{loc2}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                     \PY{n}{minD} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{min}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{minD}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n+nb}{abs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{loc1}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{n}{loc2}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{j}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
                     \PY{n}{j}\PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}
                 \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{minD}
         
         
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Your WordDistance object will be instantiated and called as such:}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} obj = WordDistance(words)}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} param\PYZus{}1 = obj.shortest(word1,word2)}
\end{Verbatim}

                 \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{m}\PY{o}{==}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{:}
                     \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{n}\PY{o}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{k}{2}==0: return (nums2[n//2\PYZhy{}1]+nums2[n//2])*0.5
                     \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:} \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{nums2}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{/}\PY{o}{/}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{*}\PY{l+m+mf}{1.0}
                 \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} if m+n is even: i+j=m\PYZhy{}i+n\PYZhy{}j \PYZhy{}\PYZgt{} j = (m+n)/2\PYZhy{}i}

                 \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} nums1[i\PYZhy{}1]\PYZlt{}=nums2[j] and nums1[i]\PYZgt{}=nums2[j\PYZhy{}1]}

                 \PY{n}{high}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{m}
                 \PY{k}{while} \PY{n}{low}\PY{o}{\PYZlt{}}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{high}\PY{p}{:}
                     \PY{n}{i} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{low}\PY{o}{+}\PY{n}{high}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{/}\PY{o}{/}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}
                     \PY{n}{j} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{m}\PY{o}{+}\PY{n}{n}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{/}\PY{o}{/}\PY{l+m+mi}{2} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{i}
                     \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{i}\PY{o}{\PYZgt{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{0} \PY{o+ow}{and} \PY{n}{nums1}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{\PYZgt{}}\PY{n}{nums2}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{j}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{:}
                         \PY{n}{high} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{i}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}
                     \PY{k}{elif} \PY{n}{i}\PY{o}{\PYZlt{}}\PY{n}{m} \PY{o+ow}{and} \PY{n}{nums1}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{n}{nums2}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{j}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{:}
                         \PY{n}{low} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{i}\PY{o}{+}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}
                     \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
                         \PY{n}{left\PYZus{}max} \PY{o}{=} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{n+nb}{float}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{inf}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
                         \PY{n}{right\PYZus{}min} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{float}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{inf}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}

                 \PY{n}{low} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}
                 \PY{n}{high} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{n}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}
                 
                 \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{find\PYZus{}rotate\PYZus{}index}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{nums}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                     \PY{n}{low} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}

                     \PY{k}{while} \PY{n}{low} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}}\PY{n}{high} \PY{o+ow}{and} \PY{n}{nums}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{low}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{==}\PY{n}{nums}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{high}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{:}

                     \PY{k}{while} \PY{n}{low}\PY{o}{\PYZlt{}}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{high}\PY{p}{:}
